    gene_name VARCHAR(50),
    chromosome VARCHAR(10),
    start_position INT,
    end_position INT
);

CREATE TABLE protein_info (
    protein_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    protein_name VARCHAR(50),
    gene_id INT REFERENCES gene_info(gene_id),
    length INT,
    sequence TEXT
);

    phenotype_id INT PRIMARY KEY,

);
